--
--	This script is designed to be run as a SQL*Plus script.
--	Do not cut this and paste into SQL*Plus as it will not work.
--	Save this to a working directory and use the SQL*Plus START command (@) to execute.
--	This script will create an .html file that can be viewed with a web browser.
--
--  If you syntax requires <org_id> and you are non-multiorg then use 0.
--
--  Use this script as requested by Oracle Support.
--  If support sends a new copy please always use the newer version.
--
--  This script can be very slow if run over a dial up line (client/server).
--  If at all possible run native on the database server.
--

undefine l_last_update
define l_last_update = '08-JAN-2004 13:40'

--
--- *** AR_Trx........... Syntax:  @ovc AR_Trx <Customer_Trx_ID> <Org_id>

--  *** AR_Auto_Indexs... Syntax:  @ovc AR_Auto_Indexs 0 0

--                        Prints all products installed on a machine.
--  *** SQL_Running...... Syntax:  @ovc SQL_Running <run number> 0
--                        Shows all SQL currently active on the database
--                        Since this is only useful if run a number of times you
--						  need to feed it a run number so it saves to new filenames each time.
--  *** SQL_Open......... Syntax:  @ovc SQL_Open <run number> 0
--                        Shows all cursors currently open on the database
--                        Since this is only useful if run a number of times you
--						  need to feed it a run number so it saves to new filenames each time.
--- *** Table Row Count.. Syntax:  @ovc Table_Size <schema> 0
--                        Shows information about each table within a schema.
--  *** Estimate......... Syntax:  @ovc Estimate 0 0
--                        Runs an estimate statistics for all tables in the schema for which it is run.

--                        Compiles all Invalids Packages and Views
--                        There is not output for this option.

set echo off
set define _
set define &
set serveroutput on size 1000000
set trimspool on
set trimout on
set verify off
set pagesize 0
set linesize 9999
set heading off
set feedback off
set timing off

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************
Prompt Enter Parameter 1 (Please check the instructions from your analyst - @ovc <param1> <param2> <param3>):
set termout off
Prompt &&1
set termout on
Prompt Enter Parameter 2 (Please check the instructions from your analyst - @ovc <param1> <param2> <param3>):
set termout off
Prompt &&2
set termout on
Prompt Enter Parameter 3 (Please check the instructions from your analyst - @ovc <param1> <param2> <param3>):
set termout off
Prompt &&3
set termout on
-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Setting Client Info Organization ID....

declare
	hold_third_parameter	varchar2(60);
begin
	hold_third_parameter := '&&3';
	if rtrim(translate(hold_third_parameter,'0123456789','          ')) is null then
		dbms_application_info.set_client_info(hold_third_parameter);
	end if;
-- If there is ever a need to go against the views that use more than just the org_id then
-- new parameters will need to be added and fnd_global.apps_initialize will need to be called.
-- This will set responsibility and userid.
end;
/

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Setting SQL*Plus Variables....

set termout off

undefine a_file_name
undefine hold_table_name
undefine hold_seq_name
undefine links_table_name
undefine ovc_package_name
undefine l_instance_name
undefine view_view_name
undefine l_app_version

define l_app_version = ''
column lappversion new_value l_app_version
select substr(release_name,1,4) lappversion from FND_PRODUCT_GROUPS where rownum = 1;

define l_instance_name = ''
column linstancename new_value l_instance_name
select substr(rpad(value,4,'_'),1,4) linstancename from v$parameter where name = 'db_name';

define hold_table_name = ''
column holdtablename new_value hold_table_name
select substr(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace('ovcx_&&l_instance_name._hld_&&1._&&2._&&3','.','_'),'$','_'),'+','_'),' ','_'),'%','_'),'~','_'),'/','_'),'-','_'),1,30) holdtablename from dual;

define hold_seq_name = ''
column holdseqname new_value hold_seq_name
select substr(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace('ovcx_&&l_instance_name._seq_&&1._&&2._&&3','.','_'),'$','_'),'+','_'),' ','_'),'%','_'),'~','_'),'/','_'),'-','_'),1,30) holdseqname from dual;

define links_table_name = ''
column linkstablename new_value links_table_name
select substr(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace('ovcx_&&l_instance_name._tar_&&1._&&2._&&3','.','_'),'+','_'),'$','_'),' ','_'),'%','_'),'~','_'),'/','_'),'-','_'),1,30) linkstablename from dual;

define view_view_name = ''
column viewviewname new_value view_view_name
select substr(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace('ovcx_&&l_instance_name._view_&&1._&&2._&&3','.','_'),'+','_'),'$','_'),' ','_'),'%','_'),'~','_'),'/','_'),'-','_'),1,30) viewviewname from dual;

define a_file_name = ''
column afilename new_value a_file_name
select substr(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace('ovcx_&&l_instance_name._&&1._&&2._&&3','.','_'),'+','_'),'$','_'),' ','_'),'~','_'),'%','_'),'/','_'),'-','_'),1,25) || '.html' afilename from dual;

set termout on

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Dropping Temporary tables...
Prompt  ......................... &&hold_table_name
Prompt  ......................... &&links_table_name

declare
	cursor_string 	varchar2(12000)  default null;
	v_cursor_id	number;
	v_dummy		integer;
begin
	begin
		cursor_string := 'drop table &&hold_table_name';
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
	begin
		cursor_string := 'drop table &&links_table_name';
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
end;
/

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Creating Temporary tables.....
Prompt  ........................ &&hold_table_name
Prompt  ........................ &&links_table_name

create table &&links_table_name (
	table_name		varchar2(60),
	table_alias		varchar2(60),
	group_cat		varchar2(60),
	where_clause	varchar2(2000),
	order_by_clause	varchar2(300),
	display_longs	varchar2(1),
	only_spaces     varchar2(1),
	view_desc1		varchar2(2000),
	view_desc2		varchar2(2000),
	view_desc3		varchar2(2000))
pctfree 0
storage (initial 10K);

create table &&hold_table_name (a long, b number)
storage (initial 10K next 10K);

create sequence &&hold_seq_name increment by 1;

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Inserting into Links Table....&&links_table_name
Prompt   ..... AR
begin
if upper('&&1') in ('AR_TRX', 'ARI_TRX') then
-- ************************
-- *** AR_Trx........... Syntax:  @ovc AR_Trx <Customer_Trx_ID> <Org_id>
-- *** ARi_Trx.......... Syntax:  @ovc AR_Trx <Customer_Trx_ID> <Org_id>
-- ************************
insert into &&links_table_name values ('RA_CUSTOMER_TRX_ALL',            Null,                   '&&1',       'where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('RA_CUSTOMER_TRX_LINES_ALL',      Null,                   '&&1',       'where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', 'line_number', 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
--insert into &&links_table_name values ('TAX_LINES_CREATE_V',      	 Null,                   '&&1',       'where trx_header_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('RA_CUST_TRX_TYPES_ALL',          Null,                   '&&1',       'where (cust_trx_type_id, nvl(org_id,999999999)) in^(select cust_trx_type_id, nvl(org_id,999999999) from ra_customer_trx_all where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`''))', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('AR_PAYMENT_SCHEDULES_ALL',       Null,                   '&&1',       'where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('RA_CUST_TRX_LINE_GL_DIST_ALL',   Null,                   '&&1',       'where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('AR_REVENUE_ADJUSTMENTS_ALL',     null,                   '&&1',       'where REVENUE_ADJUSTMENT_ID in (select revenue_adjustment_id from ra_cust_trx_line_gl_dist_all where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`''))', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('AR_ADJUSTMENTS_ALL',             Null,                   '&&1',       'where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('AR_RECEIVABLE_APPLICATIONS_ALL', Null,                   '&&1',       'where applied_customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')^or customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);
insert into &&links_table_name values ('Select',         'Application Totals',                   '&&1',       null, null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, 'select application_type, sum(amount_applied) sum_amount_applied from ar_receivable_applications_all where applied_customer_trx_id in (''&&2'') or customer_trx_id in (''&&2'') group by application_type');
if nvl('&&l_app_version','10.7') = '11.5' then
	insert into &&links_table_name values ('AR_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL',   null,                   '&&1',       'where (source_table = ''ADJ''^and source_id in^(select adjustment_id from ar_adjustments_all where customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')))'
	                                                                                                      || '^or^(source_table = ''RA''^and (source_id,org_id) in^(select receivable_application_id, org_id from ar_receivable_applications_all where applied_customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')^or customer_trx_id in (''`gk`'')))', null, 'Y', 'N', null, null, null);

Prompt  Creating HTML file...

<<main_Package>>
declare

procedure line_out (output_string long, first_time char default 'N') is
	l_long             long;
	cursor_string 	   varchar2(1000)  default null;
	v_cursor_id	       number;
	v_dummy		       integer;
	error_position     number;
	error_position_end number;
begin
	if first_time = 'Y' then
		l_long := output_string || '<!--';
	elsif first_time = 'L' then
		l_long := '-->' || output_string;
	else
		l_long := '-->' || output_string || '<!--';
	end if;
	cursor_string := 'insert into &&hold_table_name values (:tl, &&hold_seq_name..nextval)';
	v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
	DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
	DBMS_SQL.BIND_VARIABLE(v_cursor_id, ':tl', l_long);
	v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
	DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
--			line_out('</table>');
			error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
			dbms_output.put_line('Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || ' Cursor - Position: ' || error_position);
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
end;

procedure clean_invalids is
	cursor acur(v_round number) is
		select distinct object_name
		     , object_type
			, decode(object_type,'VIEW','VIEW','TRIGGER','TRIGGER','PACKAGE') my_type
			, decode(object_type,'VIEW',null,'TRIGGER',null,decode(v_round,1,' SPECIFICATION',' BODY')) my_trail
		  from user_objects
           where status = 'INVALID'
		   and object_type like decode(v_round,2,'VIEW',3,'TRIGGER','PACK%');
	l_error_flag 		 varchar2(60);
	v_cursor_id	      number;
	l_counter			 number;
begin
	for l_counter in 1..4 loop
		for a in acur(l_counter) loop
			begin
				l_error_flag := null;
				v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
				begin
					DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, 'alter ' || a.my_type || ' ' || a.object_name || ' compile' || a.my_trail , DBMS_SQL.V7);
				exception
					when others then
						l_error_flag := ' with errors - ORA-' || SQLCODE;
				end;
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
				dbms_output.put_line('Compiled ' || a.object_type || ' ' || a.object_name || l_error_flag);
				commit;
			exception
				when others then
					dbms_output.put_line('Exception for ' || a.object_name);
					dbms_output.put_line('Error: ORA' || SQLCODE);
				    	DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
			end;
		end loop;
	end loop;
end;

procedure display_profiles (application_id varchar2, debug varchar2) is
		cursor_string 				varchar2(4000)  default null;
		v_cursor_id	    	    	number;
		v_dummy						integer;
		hold_profile_id 			number;
		hold_level_id 				number;
		error_position number;
		error_position_end number;
		l_profile_option_name		varchar2(100);
		l_user_profile_option_name  varchar2(100);
		l_level_id 					number;
		l_nrows 					number;
		l_lrows 					number;
		l_a_level					varchar2(100);
		l_a_name 					varchar2(100);
		l_profile_option_id 		number;
		l_profile_option_value 		varchar2(200);
		l_creation_date 			varchar2(20);
		l_created_by 				varchar2(100);
		l_last_update_date 			varchar2(20);
		l_last_updated_by 			varchar2(100);
begin
	 	cursor_string :=     'select a.profile_option_name'
		     		|| chr(10) || ', b.USER_PROFILE_OPTION_NAME'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', c.level_id'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', k.nrows'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', j.lrows'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', decode(to_char(c.level_id),''10001'',''Site'''
			 		|| chr(10) || '                            ,''10002'',''Application'''
					|| chr(10) || '						       ,''10003'',''Responsibility'''
					|| chr(10) || '						       ,''10004'',''User'''
					|| chr(10) || '						       ,''Unknown'') a_Level'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', decode(to_char(c.level_id),''10001'',''Site'''
			 		|| chr(10) || '                            ,''10002'',nvl(h.application_short_name,to_char(c.level_value))'
			 		|| chr(10) || '                            ,''10003'',nvl(g.responsibility_name,to_char(c.level_value))'
					|| chr(10) || '				               ,''10004'',nvl(f.user_name,to_char(c.level_value))'
					|| chr(10) || '						       ,''Unknown'') a_Name'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', c.profile_option_id'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', c.PROFILE_OPTION_VALUE'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', to_char(c.CREATION_DATE, ''DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI'') creation_date'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', nvl(e.user_name,to_char(c.created_by)) created_by'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', to_char(c.LAST_UPDATE_DATE, ''DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI'') last_update_date'
			 		|| chr(10) || ', nvl(d.user_name,to_char(c.last_updated_by)) last_updated_by'
				|| chr(10) || 'from fnd_profile_options a'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_PROFILE_OPTIONS_TL b'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_PROFILE_OPTION_VALUES c'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_USER d'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_USER e'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_USER f'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_RESPONSIBILITY_TL g'
				|| chr(10) || '   , FND_APPLICATION h'
				|| chr(10) || '   , (select count(*) lrows, application_id, profile_option_id, level_id'
				|| chr(10) || '        from fnd_profile_option_values'
				|| chr(10) || '	   group by application_id, profile_option_id, level_id) j'
		   		|| chr(10) || ', (select count(*) nrows, application_id, profile_option_id'
		   	    || chr(10) || 'from fnd_profile_option_values'
			    || chr(10) || 'group by application_id, profile_option_id) k'
				|| chr(10) || 'where to_char(a.application_id) in (''' || replace(display_profiles.application_id,',',''',''') || ''')'
				|| chr(10) || '  and a.profile_option_name = b.profile_option_name'
				|| chr(10) || '  and a.profile_option_id = c.profile_option_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and a.application_id = c.application_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and a.application_id = k.application_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and a.profile_option_id = k.profile_option_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.application_id = j.application_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.profile_option_id = j.profile_option_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.level_id = j.level_id'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.last_updated_by = d.user_id (+)'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.created_by = e.user_id (+) '
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.level_value = f.user_id (+)'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.level_value = g.responsibility_id (+)'
				|| chr(10) || '  and c.level_value = h.application_id (+)'
				|| chr(10) || '  and b.language = ''US'''
				|| chr(10) || 'order by 2, 3, 5';
	v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
	if debug != 'S' then
		begin
			DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 1, l_profile_option_name, 100);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 2, l_user_profile_option_name, 100);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 3, l_level_id);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 4, l_nrows);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 5, l_lrows);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 6, l_a_level, 100);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 7, l_a_name, 100);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 8, l_profile_option_id);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 9, l_profile_option_value, 200);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 10, l_creation_date, 20);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 11, l_created_by, 100);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 12, l_last_update_date, 20);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 13, l_last_updated_by, 100);
			v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
			line_out('<font size=+2 color=purple>Profiles (Combined Display)</font>');
			line_out('<br>');
			line_out('<table border=1>');
			line_out('<tr>'
		            || '<td align=center>Long<br>Name</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Profile<br>ID</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Short<br>Name</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Level</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Level<br>Description</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Profile<br>Value</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Create<br>Date</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Created<br>By</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Updated<br>Date</td>'
		            || '<td align=center>Updated<br>By</td>'
		            || '</tr>');
			hold_profile_id := -9999;
			loop
				if DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id) = 0 then
					DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
					exit;
				end if;
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 1, l_profile_option_name);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 2, l_user_profile_option_name);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 3, l_level_id);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 4, l_nrows);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 5, l_lrows);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 6, l_a_level);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 7, l_a_name);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 8, l_profile_option_id);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 9, l_profile_option_value);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 10, l_creation_date);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 11, l_created_by);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 12, l_last_update_date);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 13, l_last_updated_by);
				line_out('<tr>');
				if hold_profile_id != l_profile_option_id then
					line_out('<td nowrap rowspan=' || l_nrows || '>' || l_user_profile_option_name || '</td>');
					line_out('<td nowrap rowspan=' || l_nrows || '>' || l_profile_option_id || '</td>');
					line_out('<td nowrap rowspan=' || l_nrows || '>' || l_profile_option_name || '</td>');
					hold_level_id := -9999;
				end if;
				if hold_level_id != l_level_id then
					line_out('<td nowrap rowspan=' || l_lrows || '>' || l_a_level || '</td>');
					hold_level_id := l_level_id;
				end if;
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_a_name || '</td>');
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_profile_option_value || '</td>');
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_creation_date || '</td>');
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_created_by || '</td>');
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_last_update_date || '</td>');
				line_out('<td nowrap>' || l_last_updated_by || '</td>');
				line_out('</tr>');
				hold_profile_id := l_profile_option_id;
			end loop;
		exception
			when others then
				error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
				line_out('<hr><font size=+2 color=red>Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || '</font>');
				line_out('<br>Position: ' || error_position  || ' of ' || length(cursor_string) || '<br>');
				line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,1,error_position),chr(10),'<br>'));
				error_position_end := instr(cursor_string,' ',error_position+1) - error_position;
				line_out('<font color=red>' || replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+1, error_position_end),chr(10),'<br>') || '</font>');
				line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+error_position_end+1),chr(10),'<br>') || '<br>');
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
		end;
	end if;
	line_out('</table><hr>');
end;

procedure table_size (target_schemas varchar2, debug varchar2) is
	cursor_string 	varchar2(1000)  default null;
	v_cursor_id	      number;
	v_dummy		integer;
	v_cursor_id_2      number;
	cursor_string_2 	varchar2(1000)  default null;
	v_cursor_id_3	      number;
	cursor_string_3 	varchar2(1000)  default null;
	row_count		integer;
	total_rows		integer := 0;
	error_position	integer;
	hold_table_name	varchar2(100);
	total_tables	integer := 0;
	hold_owner		varchar2(100);
	hold_extents	integer;
	total_extents	integer := 0;
	hold_max_extents	integer;
	hold_next_extent	integer;
	str_max_extents   varchar2(20);
	hold_indicies	integer;
	total_indicies	integer := 0;
	hold_triggers	integer;
	total_triggers	integer := 0;
	hold_columns	integer;
	total_columns	integer := 0;
	hold_ind_columns	integer;
	total_ind_columns	integer := 0;
	hold_constraints	integer;
	total_constraints	integer := 0;
	hold_free		integer;
	hold_tablespace_name varchar2(40);
	hold_sample_size	number;
	hold_last_analyzed	date;
begin
	line_out('<table border=1>');
	line_out('<tr>'
            || '<td align=center>Owner</td>'
            || '<td align=center>Table</td>'
	      || '<td align=center>Rows</td>');
	if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
		line_out('<td align=center>Sample<br>Size</td>'
		      || '<td align=center>Last<br>Analyzed</td>');
	end if;
	line_out('<td align=center>Extents</td>'
	      || '<td align=center>Max<br>Extents</td>'
	      || '<td align=center>Next<br>Extent</td>'
		 || '<td align=center># of<br>Columns</td>'
            || '<td align=center># of<br>Triggers</td>'
            || '<td align=center># of<br>Indicies</td>'
            || '<td align=center># of Indexed<br>Columns</td>'
            || '<td align=center># of<br>Constraints</td>'
            || '<td align=center>Tablespace</td>'
            || '<td align=center>Tablespace<br>Free</td>'
            || '</tr>');
	begin
		cursor_string_2 := 'select owner, table_name, max_extents, next_extent, tablespace_name';
		if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
			cursor_string_2 := cursor_string_2 || ', sample_size, last_analyzed';
		end if;
		cursor_string_2 := cursor_string_2 || chr(10) || 'from all_tables where owner in (''' || replace(upper(table_size.target_schemas),'"',''',''') || ''') order by owner, table_name';
		v_cursor_id_2 := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id_2, cursor_string_2, DBMS_SQL.V7);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 1, hold_owner, 100);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 2, hold_table_name, 100);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 3, hold_max_extents);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 4, hold_next_extent);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 5, hold_tablespace_name, 40);
		if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 6, hold_sample_size);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_2, 7, hold_last_analyzed);
		end if;
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id_2);
		loop
			if DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id_2) = 0 then
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_2);
				exit;
			end if;
			DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 1, hold_owner);
			DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 2, hold_table_name);
			DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 3, hold_max_extents);
			DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 4, hold_next_extent);
			DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 5, hold_tablespace_name);
			if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 6, hold_sample_size);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_2, 7, hold_last_analyzed);
			end if;
			error_position := null;
			begin
				cursor_string := 'select count(*) from ' || hold_table_name;
				if table_size.debug != 'S' then
					dbms_output.put_line('.....Generating Data For: ' || hold_table_name);
					v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
					DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
					DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 1, row_count);
					v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		            	v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id);
					DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 1, row_count);
					DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);

					begin
						cursor_string_3 := 'select count(*)'
						     || chr(10) || 'from dba_extents'
						     || chr(10) || 'where segment_name = ' || hold_table_name
                             || chr(10) || 'and owner = ' || hold_owner;
						v_cursor_id_3 := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
						DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id_3, cursor_string_3, DBMS_SQL.V7);
						DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_3, 1, hold_extents);
						v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id_3);
		            	v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id_3);
						DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_3, 1, hold_extents);
						DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_3);
					exception
						when others then
							DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_3);
							hold_extents := null;
					end;
					begin
						select count(*)
						  into hold_indicies
						  from all_indexes
                                     where table_name = hold_table_name
                                       and owner = hold_owner;
					exception
						when others then
							hold_indicies := null;
					end;
					begin
						select count(*)
						  into hold_triggers
						  from all_triggers
						 where table_name = hold_table_name
                                       and table_owner = hold_owner;
					exception
						when others then
							hold_triggers := null;
					end;
					begin
						select count(*)
						  into hold_columns
						  from all_tab_columns
						 where table_name = hold_table_name
                                       and owner = hold_owner;
					exception
						when others then
							hold_columns := null;
					end;
					begin
						select count(*)
						  into hold_ind_columns
						  from all_ind_columns
						 where table_name = hold_table_name
                                       and table_owner = hold_owner;
					exception
						when others then
							hold_ind_columns := null;
					end;
					begin
						select count(*)
						  into hold_constraints
						  from all_constraints
						 where table_name = hold_table_name
                                       and owner = hold_owner;
					exception
						when others then
							hold_constraints := null;
					end;
					begin
						cursor_string_3 := 'select sum(bytes)'
						      || chr(10) || 'from dba_free_space'
						      || chr(10) || 'where tablespace_name = ' || hold_tablespace_name;
						v_cursor_id_3 := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
						DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id_3, cursor_string_3, DBMS_SQL.V7);
						DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id_3, 1, hold_free);
						v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id_3);
						v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id_3);
						DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id_3, 1, hold_free);
						DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_3);
					exception
						when others then
							DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_3);
							hold_free := null;
					end;
					if hold_max_extents < 2000000000 then
						str_max_extents := to_char(hold_max_extents);
					else
						str_max_extents := 'Unlimited';
					end if;
					line_out('<tr>'
				           || '<td>' || hold_owner || '</td>'
				           || '<td>' || hold_table_name || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || row_count || '</td>');
					if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
						line_out('<td align=right>' || hold_sample_size || '</td>'
                                    || '<td nowrap>' || to_char(hold_last_analyzed,'MM/DD/RR HH24:MI') || '</td>');
					end if;
					line_out('<td align=right>' || hold_extents || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || str_max_extents || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_next_extent || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_columns || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_triggers || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_indicies || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_ind_columns || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_constraints || '</td>'
                               || '<td>' || hold_tablespace_name || '</td>'
                               || '<td align=right>' || hold_free || '</td>'
					      || '</tr>');
					total_tables := total_tables + 1;
					total_rows := total_rows + nvl(row_count, 0);
					total_extents := total_extents + hold_extents;
					total_indicies := total_indicies + nvl(hold_indicies,0);
					total_triggers := total_triggers + nvl(hold_triggers,0);
					total_columns := total_columns + nvl(hold_columns, 0);
					total_constraints	:= total_constraints + nvl(hold_constraints, 0);
				end if;
				if table_size.debug != 'N' then
					line_out('<tr><td>' || cursor_string || '</td></tr>');
				end if;
			exception
				when others then
					line_out('</table>');
					error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
					line_out('<tr><td>Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || ' - Cursor 1 - Position: ' || error_position || '</td><td>' || cursor_string || '</td></tr>');
					DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
			end;
		end loop;
		line_out('<tr></tr><tr>'
	            || '<td>Totals</td>'
	            || '<td align=right>' || total_tables || '</td>'
                 || '<td align=right>' || total_rows || '</td>');
		if lower('&&3') = 'i' then
			line_out('<td><br></td><td><br></td>');
		end if;
          line_out('<td align=right>' || total_extents || '</td>'
                || '<td><br></td>'
                || '<td><br></td>'
                || '<td align=right>' || total_triggers || '</td>'
                || '<td align=right>' || total_indicies || '</td>'
                || '<td align=right>' || total_columns || '</td>'
                || '<td align=right>' || total_constraints || '</td>'
                || '<td><br></td>'
                || '<td><br></td>'
                || '</tr>');
	exception
		when others then
			line_out('</table>');
			error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
			line_out('<br>Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || ' - Cursor 2 - Position: ' || error_position || '<br>' || cursor_string_2);
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id_2);
	end;
	if error_position is null then
		line_out('</table>');
	end if;
	commit;
end;

procedure est_all is
	v_dummy		integer;
	v_cursor_id		number;
	cursor x is
		select table_name
		from user_tables;
begin
--			select value
--			into l_compatible
--			from v$parameter
--			where name = 'compatible';
--			if substr(rpad(l_compatible,3),1,1) = '8' then
--			 	cursor_string := cursor_string
--						  || '  and iot_type != ''IOT_OVERFLOW''';
--			end if;
	for a in x loop
		begin
			v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
			DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, 'analyze table ' || a.table_name || ' estimate statistics', DBMS_SQL.V7);
			v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
			dbms_output.put_line('analyzed table ' || a.table_name);
		exception
			when others then
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
		end;
	end loop;
end;

procedure disp_table (
            table_name      varchar2,
			table_alias	    varchar2,
			where_clause 	varchar2,
			order_by_clause varchar2 default null,
			group_key	    varchar2 default null,
			display_longs   varchar2 default 'Y',
			only_spaces     varchar2 default 'N',
			view_desc1      varchar2 default null,
			view_desc2      varchar2 default null,
			view_desc3      varchar2 default null,
			debug		    varchar2 default 'N') is

	cursor i_cur (v_table_name varchar2) is
		select column_name,
			data_type,
			data_length,
			decode(instr(column_name,'ATTRIBUTE'),0,1,2),
			nullable
		from all_tab_columns
		where table_name = upper(v_table_name)
		and owner = (select min(owner)
					from all_tab_columns
					where table_name = upper(v_table_name)
					and owner not like '%_MRC%')
		order by 4, column_id;

	error_position number;
	error_position_end number;
      row_counter	number;
	hold_debug varchar2(1);
	hold_comma	varchar2(3)	default chr(10);
	hold_length	number;
	hold_color varchar2(10);
	hold_align varchar2(20);
	cursor_string 	varchar2(30000)  default null;
	add_where varchar2(25000) default null;
	hold_string	varchar2(25000)  default null;
	hold_long long;
	hold_bgcolor varchar2(40);
	column_counter	binary_integer  default 1;
	value_counter	binary_integer  default 1;
	column_high	binary_integer  default 1;
        value_high      binary_integer  default 1;
	v_cursor_id	number;
	v_dummy		integer;
	font_color_temp_open  varchar2(20);
	font_color_temp_close varchar2(8);
	l_hold_length varchar2(20);
	l_table_name varchar2(40);

	type t_values is table of varchar2(25000)
		index by binary_integer;
	v_columns 	t_values;
	v_type	    t_values;
	v_length	t_values;
	v_values	t_values;
	v_nullable	t_values;

begin
	hold_debug := debug;

	select upper(decode(upper(disp_table.table_name),'SELECT','&view_view_name',disp_table.table_name)) into l_table_name from dual;

	if disp_table.Table_Name = 'Select' then
			cursor_string := 'create view &view_view_name as ' || view_desc1 || view_desc2 || view_desc3;
			v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
			DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end if;

	cursor_string := 'select ';

	if disp_table.only_spaces = 'Y' then
		add_where := chr(10) || 'and (1 = 2';
	end if;

	for i_rec in i_cur (l_table_name) loop
		if display_longs = 'Y' or i_rec.data_type != 'LONG' then
			if i_rec.data_type in ('CLOB','SDO_GEOMETRY') then
				null; -- yet to be implemented
			else
				v_columns(column_counter) := i_rec.column_name;
				v_type(column_counter) := i_rec.data_type;
				v_length(column_counter) := i_rec.data_length;
				v_nullable(column_counter) := i_rec.nullable;
				if i_rec.data_type in ('NUMBER') then
					cursor_string := cursor_string || hold_comma || 'to_char(' || i_rec.column_name || ')';
				elsif i_rec.data_type in ('DATE') then
					cursor_string := cursor_string || hold_comma || 'to_char(' || i_rec.column_name || ',''DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI'')';
				else
					cursor_string := cursor_string || hold_comma || i_rec.column_name;
					if disp_table.only_spaces = 'Y'
					and i_rec.data_type != 'LONG' then
	  			         add_where := add_where || chr(10) || 'or nvl(' || i_rec.column_name || ',''?'') != nvl(rtrim(ltrim(' || i_rec.column_name || ')),''?'')';
					end if;
				end if;
				hold_comma := ',' || chr(10);
				column_counter := column_counter + 1;
			end if;
		end if;
	end loop;

	if disp_table.only_spaces = 'Y' then
		add_where := add_where || ')';
	end if;

	column_high := column_counter - 1;

	cursor_string := cursor_string
			|| chr(10) || 'from ' || replace(l_table_name,'V_$','V$')
			|| chr(10) || replace(replace(disp_table.where_clause,'~',''','''),'^',chr(10));

	cursor_string := cursor_string || add_where;

	if order_by_clause is not null then
		cursor_string := cursor_string || chr(10) || 'order by ' || order_by_clause;
	else
		cursor_string := cursor_string || chr(10) || 'order by 1';
	end if;

	if column_high = 0 then
		line_out('<br><font size=+2 color=purple>' || disp_table.table_name || '</font>');
		if table_alias is not null then
			line_out('<font color=orange> - ' || table_alias || '</font>');
		end if;
		line_out(' - Not Found<br><hr>');
	else
		if hold_debug != 'S' then
			line_out('<font size=+2 color=purple>' || l_table_name || '</font>');
			if table_alias is not null then
				line_out('<font color=orange> - ' || table_alias || '</font>');
			end if;
			line_out('<br>');
			line_out('<table border=1>');
			begin
				v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
				DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);

				line_out('<tr align=center>');
				for value_counter in 1..column_high loop
					if v_type(value_counter) = 'LONG' then
						hold_length := 25000;
					else
						hold_length := to_number(v_length(value_counter));
					end if;
					DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, value_counter, hold_string, greatest(hold_length,30));
					l_hold_length := null;
					if v_type(value_counter) = 'NUMBER' then
						hold_color := 'green';
					elsif v_type(value_counter) = 'DATE' then
						hold_color := 'blue';
					elsif v_type(value_counter) = 'LONG' then
						hold_color := 'orange';
					else
						hold_color := 'red';
						l_hold_length := '(' || v_length(value_counter) || ')';
					end if;
					hold_bgcolor := null;
					if v_nullable(value_counter) = 'N' then
						hold_bgcolor := ' bgcolor=lightyellow';
					end if;
					line_out('<td nowrap' || hold_bgcolor || '><font size=-2 color=' || hold_color || '>' || v_columns(value_counter) ||'</font><br><font size=-3 color=pink>' || v_type(value_counter) || l_hold_length || '</font></td>');
				end loop;
				line_out('</tr>');

				v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);

				row_counter := 1;
				loop
					if DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id) = 0 then
						exit;
					end if;
					for value_counter in 1..column_high loop
						DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, value_counter, hold_string);
					      v_values(value_counter) := hold_string;
					end loop;
					row_counter := row_counter + 1;
					line_out('<tr>');
					for value_counter in 1..column_high loop
						hold_align := null;
						if v_type(value_counter) = 'NUMBER' then
							hold_align := ' align=right';
						end if;
						font_color_temp_open  := null;
						font_color_temp_close := null;
						hold_bgcolor := null;
						if v_type(value_counter) in ('VARCHAR2','CHAR','VARCHAR') then
							if nvl(v_values(value_counter),'x') != nvl(rtrim(ltrim(v_values(value_counter))),'x') then
								font_color_temp_open := '<font color=purple>';
								font_color_temp_close := '</font>';
								hold_bgcolor := ' bgcolor=yellow';
							end if;
						end if;
						if rtrim(v_values(value_counter)) is null then
							line_out('<td' || hold_bgcolor || '>' || chr(38) || 'nbsp;</td>');
						else
							if v_type(value_counter) = 'NUMBER' then
								line_out('<td align=right>' || replace(nvl(v_values(value_counter),chr(10)),chr(10),'<br>') || '</td>');
							else
								line_out('<td nowrap' || hold_align || hold_bgcolor || '>' || font_color_temp_open || replace(nvl(v_values(value_counter),chr(10)),chr(10),'<br>') || font_color_temp_close || '</td>');
							end if;
						end if;
					end loop;
					line_out('</tr>');
				end loop;
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
				line_out('</table>');
				line_out('<font size=-2>' || ltrim(to_char(row_counter - 1,'9999999')) || ' Rows Selected');
				line_out('<br>' || replace(replace(disp_table.where_clause,'~',''','''),'^','<br>'));
				line_out(disp_table.add_where);
				line_out('<br></font>');
				line_out('<hr>');
				dbms_output.put_line('.....' || to_char(sysdate,'HH24:MI:SS') || ' Generated Data For: ' || replace(disp_table.table_name,'_$','$') || ' - ' || disp_table.table_alias || ' - ' || ltrim(to_char(row_counter-1,'999999')) || ' rows selected');
			exception
				when others then
					line_out('</table>');
					line_out('<hr>');
					error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
					line_out('<hr><font size=+2 color=red>Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || '</font>');
					line_out('<br>Position: ' || error_position  || ' of ' || length(cursor_string) || '<br>');
					line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,1,error_position),chr(10),'<br>'));
					error_position_end := instr(cursor_string,' ',error_position+1) - error_position;
					line_out('<font color=red>' || replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+1, error_position_end),chr(10),'<br>') || '</font>');
					line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+error_position_end+1),chr(10),'<br>') || '<br>');
					hold_debug := 'N';
					DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
			end;
			commit;
		end if;
	end if;

	if disp_table.Table_Name = 'Select' then
			cursor_string := 'drop view &view_view_name';
			v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
			DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end if;

	if hold_debug != 'N' then
		line_out('<hr>' || replace(cursor_string,chr(10),'<br>') || '<br>');
	end if;
end;

procedure top_level (	group_key 	varchar2 default null,
			group_cat	varchar2 default null,
			debug 		varchar2 default 'N') is

	user_name varchar2(80);
	database_name varchar2(512);
	cursor_string 	varchar2(1000)  default null;
	v_cursor_id	number;
	v_dummy		integer;
	error_position number;
	error_position_end number;

	type g_type is record (
					  table_name &&links_table_name..table_name%type
					, table_alias &&links_table_name..table_alias%type
					, group_cat &&links_table_name..group_cat%type
					, where_clause &&links_table_name..where_clause%type
					, order_by_clause &&links_table_name..order_by_clause%type
					, display_longs &&links_table_name..display_longs%type
					, only_spaces &&links_table_name..only_spaces%type
					, view_desc1 &&links_table_name..view_desc1%type
					, view_desc2 &&links_table_name..view_desc2%type
					, view_desc3 &&links_table_name..view_desc3%type
					       );
	g_rec g_type;
	l_compatible varchar2(20);

begin
	line_out('<HTML><BODY>','Y');
	select user into user_name from dual;
	line_out('<font size=+2 color=purple>Key: ' || group_cat || '=''' || group_key || ''' - &&3</font>');
	line_out('<br>User: ' || user_name);
	line_out('<br>Date: ' || to_char(sysdate,'DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI'));
	begin
		cursor_string := 'select value from v$parameter where name = ''db_name''';
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
		DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 1, database_name, 512);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
            v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 1, database_name);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
		line_out('<br>Database: ' || database_name);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
	line_out('<br>ovc Rev: &&l_last_update.<hr>');
	if upper(top_level.group_cat) = 'TABLE_SIZE' then
		table_size(top_level.group_key,top_level.debug);
	elsif upper(top_level.group_cat) = 'ESTIMATE' then
		est_all;
	elsif upper(top_level.group_cat) = 'CLEAN_INVALIDS' then
		clean_invalids;
	else
		begin
			if upper(top_level.group_cat) = 'PROFILES' then
				display_profiles(top_level.group_key, 'N');
			end if;
			cursor_string := 'select table_name, table_alias, group_cat, where_clause, order_by_clause, display_longs, only_spaces, view_desc1, view_desc2, view_desc3' || chr(10)
			          || 'from &&links_table_name' || chr(10)
					  || 'where upper(group_cat) = upper( ''' || top_level.group_cat || ''')';
			v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
			DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, cursor_string, DBMS_SQL.V7);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 1, g_rec.table_name, 60);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 2, g_rec.table_alias, 60);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 3, g_rec.group_cat, 60);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 4, g_rec.where_clause, 2000);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 5, g_rec.order_by_clause, 300);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 6, g_rec.display_longs, 3);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 7, g_rec.only_spaces, 3);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 8, g_rec.view_desc1, 2000);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 9, g_rec.view_desc2, 2000);
			DBMS_SQL.DEFINE_COLUMN(v_cursor_id, 10, g_rec.view_desc3, 2000);
			v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
			loop
				if DBMS_SQL.FETCH_ROWS(v_cursor_id) = 0 then
					exit;
				end if;
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 1, g_rec.table_name);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 2, g_rec.table_alias);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 3, g_rec.group_cat);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 4, g_rec.where_clause);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 5, g_rec.order_by_clause);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 6, g_rec.display_longs);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 7, g_rec.only_spaces);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 8, g_rec.view_desc1);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 9, g_rec.view_desc2);
				DBMS_SQL.COLUMN_VALUE(v_cursor_id, 10, g_rec.view_desc3);
				disp_table(g_rec.table_name,
					 	g_rec.table_alias,
						replace(g_rec.where_clause,'`gk`',top_level.group_key),
						g_rec.order_by_clause,
						top_level.group_key,
						g_rec.display_longs,
						g_rec.only_spaces,
						g_rec.view_desc1,
						g_rec.view_desc2,
						g_rec.view_desc3,
						top_level.debug);
			end loop;
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
		exception
			when others then
				error_position := DBMS_SQL.LAST_ERROR_POSITION;
				line_out('<hr><font size=+2 color=red>Error: ORA' || SQLCODE || '</font>');
				line_out('<br>Position: ' || error_position  || ' of ' || length(cursor_string) || '<br>');
				line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,1,error_position),chr(10),'<br>'));
				error_position_end := instr(cursor_string,' ',error_position+1) - error_position;
				line_out('<font color=red>' || replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+1, error_position_end),chr(10),'<br>') || '</font>');
				line_out(replace(substr(cursor_string,error_position+error_position_end+1),chr(10),'<br>') || '<br>');
				DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
		end;
	end if;
	line_out('</body></HTML>','L');
end;

begin
	top_level('&&2','&&1','N');
end;
/

show err

set termout off
set echo off
set trimspool on
set trimout on
set long 25000
set longchunksize 9000
set arraysize 1

spool &&a_file_name
select a from &&hold_table_name order by b;
spool off

set termout on

-- ***************************************************************************************************
-- ***************************************************************************************************

Prompt  Dropping Temporary Tables...
Prompt  ......................... &&hold_table_name
Prompt  ......................... &&links_table_name

declare
	v_dummy		integer;
	v_cursor_id		number;
begin
	begin
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, 'drop table &&links_table_name', DBMS_SQL.V7);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
	begin
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, 'drop table &&hold_table_name', DBMS_SQL.V7);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
	begin
		v_cursor_id := DBMS_SQL.OPEN_CURSOR;
		DBMS_SQL.PARSE(v_cursor_id, 'drop sequence &&hold_seq_name', DBMS_SQL.V7);
		v_dummy := DBMS_SQL.EXECUTE(v_cursor_id);
		DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	exception
		when others then
			DBMS_SQL.CLOSE_CURSOR(v_cursor_id);
	end;
	dbms_output.put_line(rpad('*',length('&&a_file_name')+21,'*'));
	dbms_output.put_line('*** Output is in &&a_file_name ***');
	dbms_output.put_line(rpad('*',length('&&a_file_name')+21,'*'));
end;
/
